local function Exista(F, ENV)
local ENV = ENV or getgenv()
for _,v in ipairs(string.split(F, ".")) do
ENV = ENV and ENV[v] end
return ENV
end

local _1, _2, _3, _4 = tostring(math.random()), tostring(math.random()), tostring(math.random()), tostring(math.random())

makefolder(_1)
makefolder(_1 .. "/" .. _2)
writefile(_1 .. "/" .. _2 .. "/" .. _3, _4)
local _ = readfile(_1 .. "/" .. _2 .. "/" .. _3)
local Fisiere = listfiles("")
for i,v in pairs(listfiles("")) do
Fisiere[i] = v:gsub("^/", "") -- path might start with "/"
end
delfile((table.find(Fisiere, _1) and _1) .. "/" .. _2 .. "/" .. _3)
if isfile(_1 .. "/" .. _2 .. "/" .. _3) then error() end
delfolder(_1)
if isfolder(_1) then error() end
return _
end)

if not Succes or Raspuns ~= _4 then
Eroare("Unsupported Executor", "File System is not working as intended")
return
end

return ("")[_1]()

Eroare("Server Error (" .. Status ..")", "Slow down! You're being rate limited", true)

end

Eroare("Server Error (" .. Status ..")", "Vonalia might be down right now. Retry later :(", true)
return
end

local BodyJson = JsonDecode(Body)

Eroare("Server Error (" .. Status ..")", BodyJson.Error, true)
return
end

local LoadingSpin

-- Global pentru scriptul obfuscat
function Mesaj(Text, Butoane, RunLoading)
getgenv().Vonalia = false
Status.Text = Text
Cutie.Visible = Butoane or false
Copiaza.Visible = Butoane or false
Valideaza.Visible = Butoane or false
Status.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, (Butoane or RunLoading) and 40 or 120)

FreezingStatus.Visible = RunLoading

if RunLoading then
if not LoadingSpin then
LoadingSpin = true
Loading.Visible = true
coroutine.wrap(function()
while LoadingSpin do
Loading.Rotation += 4
task.wait()
end
end)()
end
else
LoadingSpin = false
Loading.Visible = false
end

task.wait()
end

-- Global pentru scriptul obfuscat
function Sfarsit()
coroutine.wrap(function()
Mesaj("<font color='#00FF00'>Loading Script..</font>")
task.wait(2)
Anim(Fundal, 0.4, {Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)})
task.wait(0.4)
ScreenGui:Destroy()
end)()
task.wait(0.2)
end

local Cooldown

local function PreValideaza()
if Cooldown then
Mesaj("<font color='#FF0000'>Don't spam the button!</font>", true)
return
end

Cooldown = true

coroutine.wrap(function()
task.wait(1)
Cooldown = nil
end)()

Mesaj("Pre-Validating..", nil, true)

local _ = readfile("Vonalia/" .. VL_Name .. "/Key.txt")
if _ ~= "" then VL_Key = _ end

local Succes, Raspuns = pcall(function()
return request({
Method = "POST",
Url = "https://beta.vonalia.com/api/v1/Valideaza/Pre",
Headers = {["Content-Type"] = "text/plain"},
Body = VL_Name .. "-" .. VL_Key})
end)

-- Request Error
if not Succes then
Mesaj("<font color='#FF0000'>Request Failed\n" .. Raspuns .. "</font>", true)
return
end

local Status = tostring(Raspuns.StatusCode)
local Headers = Raspuns.Headers
local ContentType = Headers["content-type"] or Headers["Content-Type"]
local Body = Raspuns.Body

-- HTTP Error
if not Raspuns.Success then

if Status == "429" then -- Too Many Requests
Mesaj("<font color='#FF0000'>Server Error (" .. Status ..")</font>\n" .. "Slow down! You're being rate limited", true)
return
end

if not ContentType or not ContentType:find("application/json") then
writefile("Vonalia/Errors/Unexpected.txt", Body)
Mesaj("<font color='#FF0000'>Server Error (" .. Status ..")</font>\n" .. "Vonalia might be down right now. Retry later :(", true)
return
end

local BodyJson = JsonDecode(Body)

if BodyJson.Hardware then
VL_Hardware = BodyJson.Hardware
Mesaj(BodyJson.Error, true)
return
end

Mesaj("<font color='#FF0000'>Server Error (" .. Status ..")</font>\n" .. BodyJson.Error, true)
return
end

Mesaj("Hold on! This might take a little..", nil, true)
task.wait(0.2)
Valid = true
end
